Introduction:

Hi guys , 
My name is Vishal Kharchwal and I am running for the position(s) of students president of our college. because as a Nominee for this position we want your support. So please support us.

My experience and skills:

I have experience in  student politics. Because as a student leader I represent in
1) National Student parliament for two years . And also in 
2)Vidarbha student parliament for  2 years. 
3)best debater  of student Parliament award from RTMNU. 
4) win Maharashtra youth Idol Samaj Ratna award by the hands of Amitesh Kumar sir (police commissioner )of Nagpur 
5) Win  rashtriy Samaj Seva Ratna award by the hands of honourable cabinet minister Nitin Gadkari sir. 
6)Win 50+ first prize in debate competition and  elocution competition .
7) best student award from microbiologist Society of India.
and have developed the following skills :- good orator 
leader
Having a good academic record as well as cultural record . I understand the pain of others. And always try to solve the problems of peoples.
I believe these make me an ideal candidate.

What I plan to do if elected:

If elected I would aim to:

03/04/2022, 22:40 - Nikita Mam: What is the sequence of action while firing a shot?
Ans - 4 (a) Aiming Position. On taking the aim, the firer must take the first pressure.
(b) Breathing. Just before taking an aim, breathing must be gently restrained. It is 
important to coordinate so that when the foresight comes to the point of aim, the 
breath is partially exhaled.(c) Firing. Immediately on ‚Äòcorrect aim‚Äô the second pressure will be taken 
and shot fired. For a second or two after firing, there should be no relaxation of the 
hold or movement of trigger finger or head.
(d) Follow Through. The hold and aim must be maintained until the bullet has 
left the barrel. Better still fire should allow through until the bullet has reached the 
target

17/02/2023, 12:30 - Anchal Ncc: Cadets please note 
*Please iron your uniforms properly 
*Set your Barret with proper hackle 
* Carry your ncc scarf
*Polish your belts properly so it may turn black 
*Polish your DMS 
*Cut your nails 
*Carry a white handkerchief and small  chindi  
* Carry your water bottles and your tiffins 
*Please do not wear any kind of accessories in your ears and hands 
*Be confident, be in discipline co-operate with each other .
*Wear black socks under your DMS .
* carry an extra pair of arm tittle with yourself. 
* Have some breakfast before going to the centre .
*Carry a little extra lunch for your friends staying in hostle .

Stay calm and confident. you all will make it .
